< Name>
Kyle Avelar<//Name>
< Text>
Humboldt State University has a beautiful campus situated in a redwood forest overlooking the Humboldt Bay. It's located in Arcata California which is a vibrant college town with beautiful Victorian Craftsman homes historic buildings and a wide array of unique locally owned businesses lots of fantastic restaurants. Not only does the school offer quality education leading the way some fields HSU historically has had a quality athletic program. The Lumberjacks are well supported by the community making Arcata one of the most challenging places to play in division 2 athletics a few years ago under a scandalous corrupt administration the football program was eliminated which sparked outrage throughout the region Humboldt State football had been a significant tradition every fall for The Lumberjack fans from all over Northwest California. For that reason the school lost a star in my books under the new leadership of the current president and athletic director there is hope throughout the local faithful that lumberjack football could possibly make a return back to the redwood bowl arguably one of the most beautiful football stadiums in the nation for division 2 Athletics. ONLY THE BOLD WEAR GREEN AND GOLD GO LUMBERJACKS!!!< /Text>

1406909963097</date>
< Rating>
5</Rating>
< Text>
Your experience on this campus as well as any other campus, restaurants, clubs etc are solely based upon yourself. How you react to certain aspects, people and events in your life. If you go into a place with a negative mindset you've already set yourself for a negative experience and at times without realizing it we tend to reap what we sow. It's a beautiful campus with so many redwood trees and a few pine trees. Faculty and staff are helpful and nice. If you've been aching for a change in your life and HSU has a program for your major this is the way to go. I've been living in Orange County all my life and felt like I was in desperate need of a change. It's not as big as other universities but it is very beautiful. It rains, it's cold and can be windy at times but it's a nice place to be. Some people know this campus as Hills Stairs and umbrellas, since there are plenty of hills, stairs and you'll definitely be in need of an umbrella since it rains quite often the past few days have just been a  tad chilly.
Oh if you are a athlete or a workout fanatic this is where it's at. There are many hiking trials, outdoor activities and beautiful beaches.  I currently live at Creek view and I just a mini pre workout whenever I go up that hill to my place. The Behavioral and Social Sciences Building is on the opposite side of where I live and there are stairs I have to deal with, hills and just walks to class can get you pretty warm. It might be chilly  but once you're done with those stairs or hills you'll be heating up and will take off your sweater, coat or your many layers of clothing.
There aren't really any fast food places, subway is the only one I can think of for now. It's great though, since we'll be bound to eat healthy, which reminds me of the places on campus to buy food and get your munchies satisfied.  The J is a very affordable place to eat, there's also the J Grill, Hilltop Marketplace, College Creek Market place, Giant's Cupboard, Muddy Waters, The Depot and a few more. I'll be reviewing the preceding places as soon as I can. Stay tuned. I will also update my post as soon as my second semester at HSU is over & finals are over with. If  you have any questions, comments or concerns feel free to ask. ^_^< /Text>

Before I went to States, I was advised on the kinds of university I wanted to get into. I chose a small and green university, and it all came true when I saw this school for the first time. Very green, the air was really fresh, the teachers and staff were so friendly, and most importantly, I loved my dorm, Creekview which is exactly on the top of a hill.

<Text>(Translated by Google) Humboldt State University (HSU) or Humboldt State, sometimes referred to as Humboldt, is a public university in Arcata, California. It is the northernmost campus of the California State University (CSU) system of 23 schools. The main campus, located on a hillside on the edge of the Redwood Coast Forest, offers views of Arcata, much of Humboldt Bay, and the Pacific Ocean. The town of College is located on the coast of Northern California, 8 miles (13 km) north of Eureka, 279 miles (449 km) north of San Francisco, and 654 miles (1052.51 km) north of Los Angeles famous for its natural beauty.

We love it because it's generally sparse, has a nice sandy beach, nice cliffside views, and our dog can play (on leash). <gmap_id>0x80c2bf3969d106ff:0xfa77019f6b33e966</gmap_id><Name>El Sanders</Name></record></dataset><record>
<text>I used to frequent this restaurant back when it was an Irish bar called Dillon's so when I was invited to Paloma to cover their NBA All-Star Weekend party, I was super excited to see what they had done with the space. As soon as I walked in it was immediately clear that at tremendous amount of work was put into transforming what previously felt like a sports bar into an upscale lounge with gold accents on the walls and an inviting bar that welcomes you into the space. I spent a good hour and a half in this area until someone suggested that I go take some pictures at the other bar. Other bar??? That's when I walked past some cute little booths towards the back of the room to discover that there was a whole separate bar in the back with a huge dance floor and a another Dj spinning jams! It was a pleasant surprise and once I thought about it, it made sense because I had always remembered it being a pretty large space under it's former brand. I'm pretty sure it's all new ownership and from what I can tell they've done a great job hiring a fantastic staff! Even though it was pretty busy, they were super attentive and friendly and even were willing to pose for some fun pictures! I've since been back to cover some day parties there while the atmosphere is different (eg the second bar was not being used), the staff were always super welcoming and, did I mention, very easy on the eyes!!! I will definitely be back again soon, with or without my cameras! In terms of the crowd, it really varied depending on the event. The first time I went there for the All-Star party it was mainly Los Angelenos and the 'movers and shakers' & hipster crowd. During the day you'd still get some locals, but there were definitely some added tourists who came in off the boulevard. If you decide to stop by, just remember not be blink because their outdoor signage is super low key. I've included some pictures of it of course! My favorite cocktail on the menu was most definitely 'Rosemary's Baby' and they also have a decent selection of IPA's, which I love! Food wise I would highly recommend any of their tacos! I hope this helps someone out there! It's a great place to chill and hangout whenever you're in Hollywood.<//text><resp>None<//resp>< gmap_id>

Testimony.
***************************************************************************

This place is the best. I recently put in an order for the memorial day special. The very next day, I thought of something that I wanted to add, at the very last minute; so I e-mailed NR, and Adair replied back right away. < text>
I had the Tonkotsu Miso and Ika Karaage.

The miso base wasn't very good and the noodles used felt like instant noodles.. they added greens which made the soup more bitter than it should be making it difficult to enjoy it. The pork was cooked well and was charred on the skin side for a little smoked taste which I didn't mind. The egg was just right and the green onion slices were perfect.

For the Ika Karaage, it was cooked well but seemed too few for the price. It wasn't anything special to merit the more than $5 price tag.

Overall, it wasn't too bad of an experience but I was hoping it would be worthwhile to visit considering I live nearby. I've had ramen in Japan and the station ramen shops are way better.</text>

< Review>
I definitely know a thing or two about ramen (just look at my profile picture--I was born in the land of noodles) and this the **best** ramen I have ever had.

Pictured is the Tonkotsu Black, with extra egg and corn on the left and extra spicy on the right. The broth is out if this world; it is this thick, savory, indescribably amazing base that has me wanting to drink every drop even if it coats my arteries for the rest of my life (worth it)!

Our entire meal with two bowls, three extras, two soft drinks, and a beef musubi was only about 32 dollars. The prices are very competitive.

Be warned, even at 4pm on a Sunday it was 80 percent full. If you come during dinner time, expect 30 minute wait or more. Trust me, worth it!<//Review>

<Date>1546528208377</Date><rate>4< /rate><Review>The ramen is very flavourful! Here is my breakdown:
1. Wait time: not bad at all despite the size of the place and only 2 servers!
2. Service: Awesome! There were only 2 servers and they managed it wonderfully!
3. Ramen: As mentioned, the soup is flavourful and the noodles were not too firm and not too soft.
I normally like my soup and noodles to be super hot (in temperature), so for me, I felt it wasn't hot enough. The egg was not cut like in half like you normally see, but that was a good thing as it did not mess up the yolk; however, it didn't get hot enough in the center for me.
This place also has the option for no fat in the pork slices, which is excellent! Most ramen places don't have that option.
Overall, I enjoyed their food and it hit the spot for me!<//Review>< UserId.>

<text>"Clean" is how I'd describe this ramen place.  The interior of the restaurant is very clean,  and the taste of the ramen is very clean as well!  Service ain't bad either.

I had the spicy miso ramen (Level 1).  What I liked about it is that you could control how spicy you wanted it--there was a small ball of the spicy stuff in the broth, which you could take out as soon as you had the level of heat you wanted.

Price is on par with other places.  My only complaint is that the karaage appetizer came out so quickly--which is normally not bad, but it was warm, and felt like it was under a heat lamp (I could be wrong, but it just felt like that!)  But that's a minor thing as the ramen was the star of the show.</text><resp>None< /resp>< userid>

< review>
This is my new go-to ramen spot! If you're from the area, then you know shin-sen-gumi gets wildly crowded and what's up men is personally too cramped and loud for my taste. Have eaten here several times before and the Tonkatsu Black ramen was great.  Some of the best ramen in the area. 5star worthy. Delicious rich pork flavors in the broth.  I normally get spicy paste on the side and only add a little so as not to overwhelm the pork goodness.

< Text>
I came here on the weekend with friends to try this ramen out. We came around 2PM on Saturday and there was no wait at all. There is plenty of parking in the plaza. The restaurant looks very modern and nice, with plenty of seats.

I ordered the Tonkatsu Black which was just alright. The noodles were just alright, nothing too special. I felt like they did not add enough black garlic oil, they only put a bit on top of the chashu and that was it. I feel like the oil definitely made my soup tastier but I didn't really taste a garlic taste with it. The soup was creamy and it wasn't too heavy to drink. The chashu was alright, salty and tender. I wish that this bowl came with an egg, but you have to order it as a side if you want one.

Overall, the ramen wasn't bad, it was just okay. So if you're looking for a quick ramen fix, then definitely try this one out.</Text>

<date>1556185928129</date><user>112828455244746111861<//user>< Review>
If I had to pinpoint the reason why I would come back here, it would definitely be for the service.

I wouldn't call them perfect, but they're so friendly you can't be mad at them. Every single employee had a smile on their face and that contagious attitude really kept my mood throughout my dinner.

Things I liked:
- The ramen is good. I ordered the tonkatsu black with a side of egg for $1.50. The broth was very hot and the entire bowl was delicious.
- The servers are attentive but not over-the-top. They came to refill drinks, ask if we needed anything else, etc etc.
- The California roll is a very generous serving!! The 8 rolls were very thick and had far more crab meat than rice. I love that!
- You get to choose between a small and large rice bowl or curry. The server recommended getting the large bowl because the small was not very filling, but I suggest only ordering the large bowl if it's the only thing you plan on eating. Otherwise, opt for the small.

Things I didn't like:
- The gyoza was sub-par. At the entrance of the restaurant, you'll actually get the chance to watch a video on how they prepare their gyoza, but I found that the pieces were not fried long enough. They were seared, but a little too soft for my liking. Taste-wise, they were fine, but I would pass on this for my next visit.
- The lighting in the restaurant is too bright! I know that's a bit too picky, but it kills the ambiance for me.

--
Overall, I did like my experience at Yoshiharu! Though it's certainly not an LA ramen shop, it certainly is a good contender for those in the OC area.< /Review>

I love giving places 5 stars to support their service, but to account for every aspect, in this case - price, I must provide an honest and well-rounded review. The price is a little steep for ramen, which is always understandable as a means of supporting the location; however, when ramen is available from $6-8 for a bowl at many locations, itâ€™s hard to pay upwards of $10 for a bowl. Regardless, itâ€™s pretty good ramen considering the options/wait times at other places out there. The service is excellent. Thereâ€™s one gentleman who provides exceptional service consistently - part of the reason why my father loves coming here (in addition to the 5 piece gyoza for $3 with any ramen bowl).  I forget his name, but I will update as soon as I remember. I wish there was the option to provide 4.5 stars because price does not weigh that heavily in my book, and this place checks off all the rest of my boxes. Clean, great/prompt service, low wait times, convenient deals, just a little high-priced for a bowl of ramen.< /text>

< review>
Food is good,  service is great.  This is the first ramen place I have ever been to and it did not disappoint.  The server was especially friendly and very helpful. She must have answered 12 questions with a smile.  I am visiting but if I am back in town I will most certainly come again.

I had the Tonkotsu Spicy Miso with extra noodles and extra broth.... both unnecessary as the portions are large as they are but if you do order them you get a full order of ramen to take home lol.  I also got the takoyaki.  Never had it before.  Flavor was really  good but the texture was a bit unnerving,  it looked like a hush puppy but was a little mushy on the inside and that may be how it's supposed to be, can't say since I've never had it before.
Overall very pleased.< /review>
